<br><font size=-3><font color = white><font color=#009966>Sakuya sat in the back of the academy classroom, her eyes attentively scanning the blackboard. The teacher was explaining the intricacies of chakra control, doodling concentric circles and arrows to represent flow and balance. Most of her classmates looked like they were on the verge of snoozing, but Sakuya was intrigued.

As the teacher droned on, a paper airplane glided through the air and landed on her desk. She unfolded the paper discreetly, reading the hastily scribbled message: <font color = white>&#34;This is so boring! Wanna sneak out and practice some real jutsu?&#34;</font>
